================



 Posted in **MTGO Standings**
 on October 17, 2021

* [Decklists](#decklists)
* [Standings](#standings)

Bracket
-------

**(1) Beicodegeia, 2-1**

**(4) Folero, 2-0**






 (5) Hamuda

### Finals






**(1) Beicodegeia, 2-1**
